<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапавший.html>ла́павший</a> (21701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапавший.html>ла́павший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lápavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пка</a> (6408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапа.html>ла́па</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lápa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lápka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пок</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапочка.html>ла́почка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапа.html>ла́па</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lápa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><i>(of insects or small animals)</i> leg, limb, foot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягушачий.html>лягуша́чьи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljagušáčʹi lápki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frog legs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусиный.html>гуси́ные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gusínyje lápki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">crow's feet <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">around smb's eyes — lit. goose's feet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, houndstooth (textile pattern)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kurínaja lápka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">herringbone pattern <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">seam</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кверху.html>кве́рху</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:сложить.html>сложи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podnjátʹ lápki kvérxu; složítʹ lápki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">give up; throw up the towel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задний.html>за́дних</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пках</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodítʹ na zádnix lápkax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dance attendance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">перепончатая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perepončataja <b>lápka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">webbed foot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> claw, grip, clutch, pawl, tang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">полольная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лапка.html>ла́пка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pololʹnaja <b>lápka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">weeding fork</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> curly quote (one of „ “ in Russian typography)</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапоть.html>ла́поть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lápotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапоть.html>ла́птя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапоть.html>ла́пти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лапоть.html>лапте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bast shoe, bast sandal, lapti</li>
<li>an outdated, cumbersome, awkward thing</li>
<li>ignorant, uneducated person, dropout (who might wear cheap, bast shoes)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ларь.html>ларь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">larĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lárr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest, drawer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">lår</i>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ска</a> (6892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*làska</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">caress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ска</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">láska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ск</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>caress, endearment</li>
<li>petting</li></ol>

***ласковый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a> (3594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласка.html>ла́ска</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">láskovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>affectionate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгляд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láskovyj</b> vzgljad</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>affectionate</b> glance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tender, gentle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчишка.html>мальчи́шка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">malʹčíška <b>láskovyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>tender</b> boy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tvoj <b>láskovyj</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">your <b>gentle</b> voice</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>gentle, soft, caressing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láskovyj</b> svet</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>soft</b> light</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láskovyj</b> véter</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>gentle</b> breeze</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mild, pleasant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láskovyj</b> véčer</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>pleasant</b> evening</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ласковый.html>ла́сковый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассвет.html>рассве́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láskovyj</b> rassvét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>pleasant</b> dawn</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***латвийский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:латвийский.html>латви́йский</a> (16843)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ла́твия</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Látvija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латвийский.html>латви́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">latvíjskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Latvian <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to the country Latvia as a state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:латвийский.html>латви́йский</a></b> is used to refer to the country Latvia as a state, its laws, constitution, flag, government, etc. To refer to ethnic Latvians and their language, culture, customs, traditions and so on, use <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латышский.html>латы́шский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">latýšskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:российский.html>росси́йский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rossíjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rússkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ла́твия</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Látvija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">латвиец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">latvijec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">латвийка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">latvijka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латыш.html>латы́ш</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">latýš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">латы́шка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">latýška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латышский.html>латы́шский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">latýšskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:латентный.html>лате́нтный</a> (25883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">latent</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">latēns</i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лату́нь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">latúnʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***лафа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лафа́</a> (29586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">عَلَف</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʿalaf</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fodder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">алафа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">alafa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">олафа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">olafa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">лахва́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laxvá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">лахва́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">laxvá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лафа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lafá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лафы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лафы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лаф</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> benefit; luck; enjoyment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лафа.html>лафа́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó sejčás ne žiznʹ, a <b>lafá</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">His life is like a holiday now.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
